1192026-03-08T19:53:23.704802agentmessage-
The answer.json file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Plugin Signature Verification in grafana/grafana

### Core Signature Package (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/`)

1. **`manifest.go`** — The heart of plugin manifest signing/verification. Contains `PluginManifest` struct, `readPluginManifest` (PGP clearsign decoding), `ReadPluginManifestFromFS` (reads MANIFEST.txt), `Calculate` (main signature computation), `validateManifest` (field validation + PGP check), `Verify` (OpenPGP signature verification), `verifyHash` (SHA-256 file hash verification), and `urlMatch` (root URL validation).

2. **`signature.go`** — `Validator` interface and `Validation` struct. `ValidateSignature` enforces policy: valid signatures pass, unsigned plugins are checked against the allowlist, invalid/modified are rejected.

3. **`authorizer.go`** — `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` implements the unsigned plugin allowlist. `CanLoadPlugin` allows unsigned plugins only in dev mode or if the plugin ID is in `cfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned`.

4. **`statickey/static_retriever.go`** — Hardcoded Grafana PGP public key for offline/static verification.

### Key Retrieval Chain
- `keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go` — Fetches keys from Grafana.com API, caches in KV store
- `keyretriever/retriever.go` — Selects between dynamic and static retriever
- `keystore/keystore.go` — Persistent KV store for public keys

### Configuration (Allowlist Enforcement)
- `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` — Reads `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` from INI config
- `pkg/plugins/config/config.go` — `PluginManagementCfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned`
- `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginconfig/config.go` — Builds config from settings

### Pipeline Integration
- `pipeline/validation/steps.go` —

It defines `PluginManifest` (the struct representing a plugin's MANIFEST.txt), and the `Signature` struct which implements `plugins.SignatureCalculator`. Key functions:\\n- `readPluginManifest`: decodes and verifies a PGP clearsign block from MANIFEST.txt bytes\\n- `ReadPluginManifestFromFS`: opens MANIFEST.txt from a plugin's filesystem and calls `readPluginManifest`\\n- `Calculate`: the main entry point called during plugin loading \u2014 reads the manifest, validates version/ID match, checks root URLs, and verifies all file hashes via `verifyHash`\\n- `validateManifest`: validates required manifest fields and calls `Verify` to check the PGP signature\\n- `Verify`: retrieves the public key via `KeyRetriever` and uses `openpgp.CheckDetachedSignature` to verify the PGP signature\\n- `urlMatch`: validates that the Grafana app URL matches the manifest's allowed root URLs\\n\\n**`signature.go`** defines the `Validator` interface and `Validation` struct. `ValidateSignature` enforces signature policy: valid signatures pass, unsigned plugins are checked against the allowlist via `PluginLoaderAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin`, and invalid/modified signatures are rejected with typed errors.\\n\\n**`authorizer.go`** implements `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` which enforces the unsigned plugin allowlist. `CanLoadPlugin` returns true if the plugin is signed, if dev mode is enabled, or if the plugin ID appears in `cfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned`.\\n\\n**`statickey/static_retriever.go`** provides the hardcoded Grafana PGP public key (key ID `7e4d0c6a708866e7`) used to verify plugin manifests when dynamic key retrieval is disabled.\\n\\n## Interfaces (`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`)\\nDefines the key interfaces: `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` codes `ErrorCodeSignatureMissing`, `ErrorCodeSignatureModified`, `ErrorCodeSignatureInvalid`.\\n\\n## Pipeline Integration\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`**: `DefaultConstructor.Construct` calls `signatureCalculator.Calculate` during plugin construction to compute the signature state before the plugin is created.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/factory.go`**: `DefaultPluginFactory.newPlugin` sets `Signature`, `SignatureType`, and `SignatureOrg` fields on the `Plugin` struct from the calculated signature.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`**: `SignatureValidationStep` wraps `signature.Validator.ValidateSignature` as a pipeline validation step. `DefaultValidateFuncs` wires together signature validation, module.js validation, and Angular detection.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/validation.go`**: The `Validate` stage orchestrates all validation steps.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/pipeline.go`**: `ProvideBootstrapStage` and `ProvideValidationStage` wire the signature calculator and validator into the plugin loading pipeline.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`**: Contains the integration-layer `SignatureValidation` and `SignatureValidationStep` that wrap the core validator and record errors.\\n\\n## Key Retrieval\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`**: `KeyRetriever` fetches public keys from the Grafana.com API (`/plugins/ci/keys`) and caches them in the `KeyStore`. It runs periodically (every 10 days) and can be disabled via `PluginSkipPublicKeyDownload`.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`**: `Service` selects between the dynamic
